[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/home/qqor/crete/packages/python_oss_fuzz/.oss_fuzz/build/out/[0m[95mwireshark[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m -v [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/[0m[95mtmpxdrit7h1[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m -t ghcr.io/aixcc-finals/base-runner:v1.[0m[1;36m3.0[0m[39m reproduce [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandler_telnet -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-use-after-free vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark telnet [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol dissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`packet-telnet.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during fuzzing tests. The issue occurs when [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory that has been freed is subsequently accessed through a write operation, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically during the processing of telnet suboptions. The vulnerability is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered when `telnet_add_text` attempts to access memory at address [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x51c000000880[0m[39m` that was previously freed by `telnet_sub_option`.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis issue represents a **heap-use-after-free** vulnerability with a scariness [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscore of [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m, involving a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte write operation to freed heap memory. [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerability Details:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Error Type**: AddressSanitizer detected a heap-use-after-free condition[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Operation**: WRITE of size [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Memory Address**: [0m[1;36m0x51c000000880[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwithin a [0m[1;36m1920[0m[39m-byte region[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Thread**: T0 [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmain thread[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Execution Flow:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests through the following call chain:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Memory Allocation**: Memory is initially allocated via `g_malloc` in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_naws_subopt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-telnet.[0m[1;92mc:652[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during the processing of telnet [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNegotiate About Window Size [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNAWS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m suboptions.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Deallocation**: The allocated memory is freed in `telnet_sub_option` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mpacket-telnet.[0m[1;92mc:2099[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m through `wmem_simple_free`, which occurs during the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing of telnet commands in the dissection flow [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`telnet_command` → [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`telnet_sub_option`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Use-After-Free Access**: After deallocation, the code proceeds to [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`telnet_add_text` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-telnet.[0m[1;92mc:2211[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which calls [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz` → `_tvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz` → `tvb_memcpy`. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis chain ultimately triggers `memcpy` that attempts to write to the freed memory [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Observations:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerability occurs within the telnet protocol dissector, specifically in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe handling of telnet suboptions[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The freed memory region is [0m[1;36m1920[0m[39m bytes in size[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The deallocation happens in `telnet_sub_option` before subsequent use in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`telnet_add_text`[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer input that triggered this issue is: [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m372[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m037[0m[39m\000P\[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m030[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m360[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m372[0m[39m\"\[0m[1;36m001[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m001[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\360aaaa`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The issue is reproducible with [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m fuzzing runs[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Areas for Investigation:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be examined:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **epan/dissectors/packet-telnet.c**: [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `dissect_naws_subopt` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m652[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where memory allocation occurs[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `telnet_sub_option` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2099[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where memory is freed[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `telnet_command` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2182[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that orchestrates the suboption [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `telnet_add_text` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2211[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where the freed memory is accessed[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `dissect_telnet` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2322[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2337[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m managing the overall [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissection flow[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **epan/tvbuff.c**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `tvb_memcpy` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m945[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m performing the memory copy operation[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `_tvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz` and `tvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m4047[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m4073[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that prepare data for copying[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Management Context**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The interaction between `g_malloc`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`wmem_simple_free` and the telnet [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector's memory lifecycle[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The scope and lifetime management of allocated buffers during telnet suboption[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The relationship between different telnet suboption handlers and their shared [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory resources[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability appears to stem from a lifetime management issue where memory [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated for processing one aspect of telnet suboptions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNAWS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is freed [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprematurely, but a reference or pointer to this memory is still retained and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequently dereferenced in the text addition routine.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of Code Snippets in Relation to Evaluation Report[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Insights Extracted[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause Identified**: The heap-use-after-free occurs due to improper state [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement when different telnet suboptions share global variables:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_naws_subopt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m652[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allocates memory from `pinfo->pool` and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstores pointer in global `hf_naws_data`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Sets global flag `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m655[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_linemode_subopt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m640[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m frees the memory via [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Critical Bug**: Does NOT clear the flag or null the pointer[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `telnet_add_text` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2209[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2211[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m checks the flag and attempts to write to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed memory[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Additional Vulnerabilities Found**:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Integer overflow: `hf_telnet_width * hf_telnet_height` can overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m65535[0m[39m * [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65535[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Out-of-bounds write: No validation that `start_offset` is within buffer bounds[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Architecture mismatch: Global variables storing packet-scoped memory pointers[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Non-functional feature: The window buffer is never read or displayed[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Critical Logic to Preserve**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - NAWS suboption dissection should still display width/height fields [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m659[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m661[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Linemode suboption dissection should continue to work[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Text addition functionality must remain intact [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2254[0m[39m for normal display[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The telnet option dispatch mechanism must not be disrupted[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Previous Patches**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m indicated in the evaluation report - this is the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitial fix attempt.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix Strategy[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Minimal Fix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mImmediate Patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch `dissect_linemode_subopt` to properly reset state after freeing memory:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-telnet.c`, lines [0m[1;36m635[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m643[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mdissect_linemode_subopt[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket_info *pinfo, const char *optname _U_, tvbuff_t *tvb [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m---[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Complete Removal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRecommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification for Recommended Fix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOption [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Is Optimal**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates All Vulnerabilities**: Removes use-after-free, integer overflow, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand out-of-bounds write risks[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Removes Dead Code**: The window buffer is never read or used for any purpose[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: NAWS width/height fields continue to be displayed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperly[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Architectural Correctness**: Eliminates inappropriate use of global variables [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor packet-scoped data[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Maintenance Benefit**: Simplifies codebase by removing non-functional feature[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Preserves Existing Logic**:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Telnet dissection continues normally[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- NAWS suboption still displays width and height fields[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- LINEMODE suboption dissection works unchanged[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Text display via `telnet_add_text` continues to function[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other telnet options remain unaffected[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses Issues in Evaluation Report**:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Heap-use-after-free**: Eliminated by removing the memory [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation/deallocation code[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Memory allocated at line [0m[1;36m652[0m[39m**: Allocation removed[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Memory freed at line [0m[1;36m2099[0m[39m**: Deallocation removed  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Memory accessed at line [0m[1;36m2211[0m[39m**: Access removed[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer input will no longer trigger the crash path[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects and Mitigation**:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Side Effect**: Loss of window buffer feature[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: Not needed - feature provides no value [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer never used[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Side Effect**: Users expecting window buffer data[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: Not applicable - feature was non-functional [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata never [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisplayed[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Side Effect**: Breaking existing tests[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: Unlikely - feature appears unused; if tests exist, they test [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbroken functionality[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar Solutions in Codebase**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `unescape_and_tvbuffify_telnet_option` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1095[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1129[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
